              <p

                    </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span
                  style="color:windowtext">The <b>International Journal
                    of Cloud Computing</b> and the whole <span
                    class="SpellE"><b>Inderscience</b></span><b>
                    Publishers</b> highly rated paper [40]. On September
                  15, 2015, <span class="SpellE">Inderscience</span>
                  Publishers announced the endeavor of cloud-dew
                  architecture to the science community in the form of a
                  public release. Over 30 media published the news,
                  including some media in Russia, India, Japan,
                  Montenegro, and Colombia. These media are listed <a
                    href="list.html">here</a>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

              <p class="MsoNormal"
                style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-right:179.25pt;
                margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:126.0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:





                inter-ideograph;tab-stops:538.85pt 547.85pt"><b><span
                    style="font-size:14.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt"><a
                      href="PastTeaching.htm">Teaching Profile</a><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
              <p class="MsoNormal"
                style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-right:179.25pt;
                margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:126.0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:





                inter-ideograph;tab-stops:538.85pt 547.85pt"><b><span
                    style="font-size:14.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt"><a
                      href="https://doi.org/10.31235/osf.io/u4zcs">TSINC
                      Testing Method</a><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
              <p
                style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:108.0pt;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
                margin-left:126.0pt">TSINC is a new online testing
                method. The acronym TSINC represents its five
                characteristics: Time-pressed, Sequential,
                Individualized, Not searchable, and Calibration-bound.
                Its primary feature is that it can be used to organize
                plagiarism-resistant online testing without human
                monitoring.</p>

                    </span></span></span><!--[endif]--><span
                  style="color:windowtext">The <b>International Journal

                  architecture to the science community in the form of a

              <p class="MsoNormal"

                inter-ideograph;tab-stops:538.85pt 547.85pt"><b><span
                    style="font-size:14.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt"><a
                      href="PastTeaching.htm">Teaching Profile</a><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
              <p class="MsoNormal"
                style="mso-margin-top-alt:auto;margin-right:179.25pt;
                margin-bottom:12.0pt;margin-left:126.0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:





                inter-ideograph;tab-stops:538.85pt 547.85pt"><b><span
                    style="font-size:14.0pt; mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt"><a
                      href="https://doi.org/10.31235/osf.io/u4zcs">TSINC
                      Testing Method</a><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
              <p
                style="margin-top:5.0pt;margin-right:108.0pt;margin-bottom:5.0pt;
                margin-left:126.0pt">TSINC is a new online testing
                method. The acronym TSINC represents its five
                characteristics: Time-pressed, Sequential,
                Individualized, Not searchable, and Calibration-bound.
                Its primary feature is that it can be used to organize
                plagiarism-resistant online testing without human
                monitoring.</p>
